== test_smem_back_to_back_throughput.py  (2026-04-19T00:03:31)

================================================================================
=== SCENARIO A: verbose back-to-back sh.ld -> sh.st (1 warp, no drain) ===
================================================================================
One 32-thread warp issues a full sh.ld instruction immediately followed by a full sh.st instruction. The verbose cycle dump below should show the read controller and the write controller retiring a transaction each in the same cycle, yielding ~2 txn/cycle steady state.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  A. Verbose sh.ld -> sh.st (1 warp, 2 instructions)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  Instructions issued back-to-back: 2
  Per-thread transactions:          64
  Total cycles:                     36
  Steady-state throughput:          1.778 txn/cycle
NOTE: Scenario A overlaps only the transition window between the two instructions; the bulk of each instruction still runs single-controller, so end-to-end throughput on this short chain is dominated by that phase.

================================================================================
=== SCENARIO B: pure sh.ld x 8 warp-wide instructions (256 txns total) ===
================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  B. Pure sh.ld x8 (256 txns)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  Instructions issued back-to-back: 8
  Per-thread transactions:          256
  Total cycles:                     260
  Steady-state throughput:          0.985 txn/cycle
Pure sh.ld chains can only use the SMEM read controller, which retires one request per cycle => ~1.0 txn/cycle steady state.

================================================================================
=== SCENARIO C: pure sh.st x 8 warp-wide instructions (256 txns total) ===
================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  C. Pure sh.st x8 (256 txns)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  Instructions issued back-to-back: 8
  Per-thread transactions:          256
  Total cycles:                     257
  Steady-state throughput:          0.996 txn/cycle
Pure sh.st chains can only use the SMEM write controller, which retires one request per cycle => ~1.0 txn/cycle steady state.

================================================================================
=== SCENARIO D: alternating sh.ld / sh.st x 8 pairs (16 instructions, 512 txns total) ===
================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  D. Alternating sh.ld/sh.st x8 pairs (512 txns)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  Instructions issued back-to-back: 16
  Per-thread transactions:          512
  Total cycles:                     260
  Steady-state throughput:          1.969 txn/cycle
Alternating chains let the read and write controllers each retire one request per cycle in parallel => ~2.0 txn/cycle steady state.

================================================================================
=== SCENARIO E: realistic mix LD,LD,ST,LD,ST,ST,LD,ST (8 warp-wide) ===
================================================================================

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  E. Realistic LD,LD,ST,LD,ST,ST,LD,ST (256 txns)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  Instructions issued back-to-back: 8
  Per-thread transactions:          256
  Total cycles:                     132
  Steady-state throughput:          1.939 txn/cycle
Mixed patterns fall between the 1.0 and 2.0 txn/cycle bounds depending on how many cycles have both a pending read and a pending write.

==========================================================================================
Back-to-back sh.ld / sh.st throughput summary
==========================================================================================
Scenario                                           | Instr |  Txns | Cycles |  Txn/Cyc
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
B. Pure sh.ld x8 (256 txns)                        |     8 |   256 |    260 |    0.985
C. Pure sh.st x8 (256 txns)                        |     8 |   256 |    257 |    0.996
D. Alternating sh.ld/sh.st x8 pairs (512 txns)     |    16 |   512 |    260 |    1.969
E. Realistic LD,LD,ST,LD,ST,ST,LD,ST (256 txns)    |     8 |   256 |    132 |    1.939

Expected peak:  pure sh.ld or sh.st = 1.0 txn/cyc (single controller bottleneck),
                alternating sh.ld/sh.st = 2.0 txn/cyc (read + write controllers retire one each per cycle).
